<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>и́м<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:позаимствовать.html>позаи́мствовать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-заимств-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заинтересоваться.html>заинтересова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zainteresovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересоваться.html>интересова́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become interested in (+ instrumental case)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заинтересовать.html>заинтересова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zainteresovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заинтриговать.html>заинтригова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaintrigovávšij</span>)

***зайти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зайти.html>зайти́</a> (1119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайти.html>зайти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zajtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go (to see), to come in (to see, etc.), to call, to drop in</li>
<li>to pick up, to fetch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call at, to enter (a port)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to advance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass, to draw out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to approach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to outflank</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn, to disappear, to go behind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be well received</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зайти.html>Зайти́</a></b> is a Russian concrete verb. Its counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зайц-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zajc-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайчик.html>за́йчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zájčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайчик.html>за́йчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайчик.html>за́йчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зайчик.html>за́йчиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заяц.html>за́яц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zájac</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: bunny, hare; darling, sweetheart, sunny</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reflection of a lightbeam</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>за́й<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чик</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***заказать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказать.html>заказа́ть</a> (3105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заказать.html>заказа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заказывать.html>зака́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to order, to place an order</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to forbid, to prohibit, to ban</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заказной.html>заказно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakaznój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>made to order; made to measure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of clothes and shoes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***закалка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лка</a> (22229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">закали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakalítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to temper, to harden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakálka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tempering, hardening</li>
<li>training (for endurance)
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><i>James Joyce</i> Ulysses.1914-1921:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́ннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнюю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закалка.html>зака́лку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:унаследовать.html>унасле́довав</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерзкий.html>де́рзкую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонность.html>скло́нность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инакомыслие.html>инакомы́слию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противостояние.html>противостоя́нию</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отвергать.html>отверга́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:многие.html>мно́гие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общепринятый.html>общепри́нятые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:религиозный.html>религио́зные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:национальный.html>национа́льные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:социальный.html>социа́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравственный.html>нра́вственные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доктрина.html>доктри́ны</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óba, polučív ránnjuju domášnjuju <b>zakálku</b> i unaslédovav dérzkuju sklónnostʹ k inakomýsliju i protivostojániju, otvergáli mnógije obščeprínjatyje religióznyje, nacionálʹnyje, sociálʹnyje i nrávstvennyje doktríny</i></dd><dd>both, having received early domestic <b>training</b> and inherited a pert penchant for dissent and opposition, dismissed many among generally accepted religious, national, social and moral doctrines</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
